# PHOTON ASCII

struct ORGANIC[N] {
	X
	Y
	ENERGY
}

struct BARRIER[N] {
	X
	Y
}

struct ER {
	FIDX
	RIDX
	STATE[N] {
		VALUE
	}
}

struct KFMO {
	MAX_CODE_BLOCKS
	MAX_APPLY
	PROB_MUTATE_CODEBLOCK
	PROB_DUPLICATE
	PROB_DELETE
	PROB_INSERT
	PROB_TRANSPOSE
	PROB_MODIFY
}

struct SPORE {
	X
	Y
	ENERGY
	PARENT
	STRAIN
	SFLAGS
	PROGRAM[N] {
		TEXT_LINE
	}
}

struct CELL {
	ORGANISM_ID
	X
	Y
	MOOD
	MESSAGE

	MACHINE {
		TERMINATED
		CB
		PC
		R[N] {
			VALUE
		}

		CALL_STACK[N] {
			CB
			PC
		}

		DATA_STACK[N] {
			VALUE
		}
	}
}

struct ORGANISM {
	ORGANISM_ID
	STRAIN
	OFLAGS
	PARENT1
	PARENT2
	GENERATION
	ENERGY
	AGE
	PROGRAM[N] {
		TEXT_LINE
	}
}

struct KEYLIST {
	KEY
	VALUE
}
struct PLAYER {
	TERMINATED
	X
	Y
	ENERGY
	AGE
	CMD {
		TYPE
		X
		Y
	}
}

struct UNIVERSE {
	SEED
	STEP
	NEXT_ID
	NBORN
	NDIE
	WIDTH
	HEIGHT
}
